 grahamantri rajnath singh ne pichley hafte bharat-tibet seemaa bal itibipi ke sainikon or adhikariyon kii is baat ko lekar saraahna kii thi ki unhone javaanon ke mul prashikshan main mandarin bhashaa shaamil kii he taaki piele sainikon ke saath aamanaa-saamana hone par samvaad main unhen madad mil sake
 So the Indian soldier who is learning Mandarin, quoting research fellow Hu Jiang at the Shanghai Academy of Social Sciences Institute of International, said, "india's concern over China has increased since the Doklam dispute, so it has given its soldiers the Mandarin language
 Instructed to learn so that he can communicate with the Chinese soldiers and cause misunderstandings of Bevajah
 'ek-duusare kii bhashaa-samskruti samajhane kii jarurathu jiyang ne suzav diya ki donon pakshon ke agrim pankti ke javaanon ko ek duusare kii samskruti, bhashaa or paramparaon ke bare main jaankaree leni chahie

 " hong-kong besd tech company sound van ne bharat main farvari ke maheene main apane neckband style vaale X60 wireles headphone ko launch kiya tha
 This headphone with Bluetooth connectivity is designed for both music and calls
 company ne isaki keemat 3,490 rupee rakhi he, haalanki flipcart abhi ye 1,890 rupee main uplabdh he
 We have used this headphone for a long time and now we are passing it on to you
 dizin or bild quality:is wireles headphone ke dizin kii baat karen to ye vajan main kaaphi halkaa he
 Any headband with a neckband has a problem of light and thin device
 aise main ye thik he
 It is not very premium in appearance nor is there any attraction in its packaging
 band ke upar rabar kii soft rabar kii coating kii gai he
 The design of the given button is also not much special
 yahaan left said main virtual assistant active karne ke liye van tach batan diya gaya he
 At the same time, multi-function buttons and volume buttons are provided in the ride side
 multi function batan se on-of karne samet kol cat-risive or redayal karne jaise kaam hote hai or wolum buttens main plus batan ko dabaakar rakhane se wolum badhati he or ek baar dabaane par trek change hota he
 Similarly, the negative button works in the volume buttons
 isse wolum kam hoti he
 Apart from this, they are of small design when it comes to earplugs
 aise main aasaani se kaanon main feet baith jate hai or kaanon main chubte bhi nahin hai
 But these earplugs are connected to the band with which they are very average wire
 inaki quality chune se bhi kaaphi everej lagati he or ye luk ke hisaab se bhi kaaphi nimna str kaa lagata he
 It is also possible that when pulled a bit, this wire breaks and breaks
 yahaan yearplag main drivers ke peeche ke hisse main magnet diya gaya he jo inhen upyog naa hone kii sthiti main chipkaakar rakhata he
 However, these magnets do not perform any other function like earplugs magnets of other companies
 parformens or audio quality:sabase pehle connactivity kii baat karen to yahaan bluetooth 4
 Support of 2 is provided
 aise main ye smartphone, computer or audio players ke liye kaaphi compatible he
 Also, there is no problem in connectivity
 auto connactivity hone kii vajah se headphone aasaani se smartphone se conect bhi ho jaataa he
 Its connectivity range is up to 10m which is better
 ab audio quality kii baat karen to Sound One X60 kii range 20-20,000hz tak he
 Also, Qualcomm's aptx codec technology has also been used for better quality here
 baharhaar audio quality kii baat karen to hamane is headphone main kaaphi tarah ke mujeec jaise- clasical, rock, jaij, regeton, deep house, ecostic, EDM, trans or dabstep ko headphone se suna or paaya ki ye Lows yani ye base ke liye behatar he
 At the same time, Mids and Highs are quite weak
 yani aap yahaan everej sound quality kaa anand le paaenge
 Here you will not feel base and you will clearly find a lack of crisp in the rest of the music
 haalanki acchhee baat ye he ki aapako aawaaj puri tarah badhaane ke baad bhi koi kharaab aawaaj kaa saamana nahin karnaa hoga
 After this, if you talk about the voice button, it works fine
 in sabake baad colling kii baat karen to yahaan ye headphone tarif batorne ke laayak he
 Because you will get a lot of clarity in calling as well, connectivity will also get better and you will not be disturbed by any kind of external noise
 bydaree:ant main bydaree parformens kii baat karen to company ke daawey ke mutabik ise single charge main 8 se 10 ghante tak chalaaya ja saktaa he or yahaan company kaa daawa sahi he
 We did not face any problem with the battery
 saath hi ise charge karne main 2 ghante kaa samay lagata he
 One bad thing is that this headphone gives you continuous ring alert as soon as the battery is 20 percent, in such a situation, you can get upset while watching any music or video in low battery

 - input bhashaa The death of veteran South African leader 'bharat Ratna' Nelson Mandela, who waged a historic struggle against apartheid, has triggered a wave of mourning across the world
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh, america raashtrapati baraak obama, abhinayta amitabh bachchan samet raajnneeti, film or saamaajik jagat kii rashtriya or antarrashtriya hastiyon ne mandela ko shradhanjali arpit kii he
 The flag of the country has been tilted until the last farewell ceremony in South Africa
 insaanon ke bich mahaan shaks tha wo: mandelapradhanmantri ne bayaan jari kar kaha, 'ishwar, yahaan-vahaan, jab-tab, insaanon ke bich kuch mahaan logon ko banaata he
 Mandela was one of them 
 mandela lade taaki duusare log samanta, avasar or gaurav ke saath ji saken
 'the Prime Minister said that Mandela has raised the value of India by accepting' Bharat Ratna ', the country's greatest civilian honor
 vah sachche gandhivadi the
 Their departure is a tremendous loss for India, South Africa and the whole world
 'raashtrapati or modi ne bhi jataayaa shokarashtrapati pranab mukherjee ne bhi shok sandesh jari kar kaha he ki mandela maanavtaa kii prerana the
 bjp's Prime Ministerial candidate and Gujarat Chief Minister Narendra Modi wrote on Twitter, 'many of us did not get the privilege of seeing Gandhiji alive
 lekin ham khushnaseeb hai ki ham nelson mandela ke jivan ke gavaah bane
 We have lost a symbol of non-violence and peace
 'maine lee mandela se prerana: obamakhud ko mandela se prerana lene vaale lakhon logon main se ek bataate hue america raashtrapati baraak obama ne bhi unke nidhan par shok jataayaa or kaha ki duniya ko unke jaisaa netaa dobaaraa nahin mil saktaa
 The US president said, 'my first political act - the first thing i ever associated with any policy, issue or politics was opposition to apartheid
 ek kaidi se lekar raashtrapati tak kaa unka safar yah vaada karata he ki insaan or desh behatar tabdili laa sakate hai
 'every country is sad today, Prince William of Britain also paid tribute to Mandela and said that his contribution cannot be forgotten
 britain ke pradhanmantri david camerun ne kaha ki mandela ne kai deshon ko shantipurna andolan kii prerana di
 In London, Mandela's daughter Jindji said that her father was well until a day earlier
 'madiba' ke naam se mashhoor mandela lambey samay se fefdon ke sankraman se jujh rahe the
 The United Nations also mourned the death of Mandela and said that the world's most popular leader was no more
 australia ke pradhanmantri toni aboch ne unhen yaad karte hue sadi kaa sabase bade netaa bataaya he
 Amitabh shared his and Mandela's death on Facebook and Twitter also led to a flood of mourning messages
